pa'i mkhyen brtse nus pa'i spyi gzugs mkhas pa dang grub pa'i

nyid gchog(sic!) gsum gyi thugs rje dang lus can spyi mthun gyi

rnying ma yon tan mgon po slar yang bsam bzhin du srid pa bzung

ba dang/ gso ba rig pa'i bstan pa rin po che nyin mo ltar gsal

dkon cog bde legs byams pa bde legs tel

/ gangs can mkhas pa'i gtsug rgyan zhes bya Inga/
I gsang sngags rnying ma'i bstan pa la zhugs nas/

gsungs pas/ de Inga'i ring la sman 'phreng sman sgrub sogs

/ skye ba bzhes pa'i skyes bu dam pa ni/

G.yu-thog II
dus babs la/

/'gro ba sems can snyigs ma la dgongs nas/
/g.yu thog gsar ma zhes byar rab grags pa/

/ sman 'phreng sman sgrub nyams len rgyas par byed) /ces
gsungs so

zhang po khungs 1dan btsal/ /zhes pa ltar/ 'di'i cho 'brang ni

G.yu-thog II
pas de rdzi bo zhig gis mthong bas rdzi bo na re sgo bzhi re

mtho gang tsam zhig yum rang gi snying kha'i thad du 'dug pa'i

ma tshogs 'khor gshom zhig/ 'dod don sgrub po gsungs/

ngan sngags bzlog pa'i 'khor lo/ sman gyi sa bon thebs pa'i
'khor lo/ 'bras bu smin pa'i 'khor lo mnams gnang ngo/
de nas a tsa ras lho phyogs sogs phyogs bzhi la sdigs
mdzub gtad pas/ phyogs bzhi nas sha chang la sogs pa'i zas kyi
bye brag sna tshogs dang/ sman dang bdud rtsi la sogs pa bsam
gyis mi khyab pa 'dus byung bas/ a tsa ras tshogs byin rlabs
mdzad pas/ bdud rtsi kha dog Inga ldan du gyur song ngo/
1 /sang nyin de dā ma ru'i sgra dang tshil chom gyi sgra
chen po byung bas/ a tsa ra'i zhal nas yid 'phrog ma mchod pa
gshom zhig/ drang srong chen po dang bram ze chen po 'byon par
gda' gsung/ yid 'phrog mas mchod pa gshams nas gzigs pas khong
(f. 13r)

G.yu-thog
I
brten/ yul padma'i snying po na rgyal po utpa la'i gdong btsun
mo dang blon po'i tshogs dpag tu med pas bskor nas yod pa'i tshe/
srin po'i dmag bcug go/
de nas yid 'phrog mas rgyal po la g.yul las rgyal bar byed
pa'i bsring ba dang 'khor lo btags/ blon po gzhan mams la g.yul
bzlog pa dang/ g.yul bsrung ba dang/ g.yul bskrad pa'i 'khor lo
btags/ blon po blo gros chen po la rgyal po 'dzin pa dang/ rgyal
po being ba'i 'khor lo dang/ drang srong chen po'i dbu skra
gsum sgril la bcos pa'i thag pa bskur/ blon po gser chen po la
blon po 'dzin pa dang bcing ba'i 'khor 10/ drang srong chen
po'i dbu skra la bcos pa'i thag pa mnams bskur ro/
/rgyal bu dga' ba'i blo gros la dmag mi bcing ba dang bskrad
pa'i 'khor lo btags te/ yid 'phrog ma rang gi gang bsam 'grub
pa'i 'khor lo bskor nas/ srin po dang g.yul bkye bas srin po
mams ni mgo bo dang lag pa mang po 'dug cing/ srin po'i rgyal
po la mgo bo nyi shu rtsa gcig/ lag pa bzhi bcu zhe gnyie/ phyag
mtshan mda' gzhu dang zhags pa dang/ sta re ral gri mdung la
sogs pas brgyan pa 'dug gol
/srin po'i blon po khyab ba lag ring bya ba la mgo bcu
gcig lag pa nyi shu rtsa gnyis/ phyag mtshan rgyal po dang 'dra
ba 'dug go!
/rgyal po utpa la'i gdong dang rgyal bu dga' da'i blo gros
kyis btsan sa srin po'i gnod pa mi yong ba zhig tu yid 'phrog
ma'i bslabs pa'i 'khor lo bakor gyin bzhugs/ blon po blo gros
chen po dang/ blon po (f. 19r)



po gser chen pos amag dpon byas g.yul bkye bas/ blon po blo
gros chen po la srin po'i rgyal pos mtshon cha bskor bas/ blon
po blo gros chen pos drang srong chen po'i dbu skra la bzos
pa'i thag pa dbyug pas/ srin po'i rgyal. po'i mgo bo bcu yar
bzhag bcu mar bzhag pa'i dbus na seng ge'i mgo bo gcig 'dug
pa de'i gdong pa'i nyag la thebs so/

ma la ya nas gangs can bar mtshams na/

G.mu-thog I
srong rigs 'dzin lha mo/ dar byed kun tu grags pa'i sman pa

gsungs nas gso2 ba 'di skad btab bo/

nas/ bram ze ma nad kyis btab pa'i lo rgyus zhus pas/ drang

dkar po/
1ha yul sum au rtsa gsum bdag po stel

so/

/'di dag sman ni yan lag brgyad/

/bsdu na sman dpyad zas spyod bzhi/ /gsungs so/
/de nas gru gu'i sman pa na re/ gso ba rig pa spyi'i dpe
de mams/ rgya gar rgya nag bal po kha che sog po dol po gru
gu khrom sogs sde rigs mi 'dra tha dad du/ sman pa la snga bal
rgyal po la snga ba sus blangs zer rol
/de nas g.yu thog chen pos 'di skad gsungs solo
/dpe de mams rgya gar du rgyal po rta mchi can gyi ring
la/ bram ze 'i sman pa ha la mig yangs kyis blangs/
rgya nag tu rgyal po seng pags can gyi ring Ia sman pa ha
la dha ras blangs/
hor du rgyal po 'baº gdur gyi ring la sman pa 'bi gu tas
blangs/

dpal gyis blangs/

blangs/
gar log tu rgyal po ga ga'i ring la sman pa ha ri snas

ta zig tu rgyal po bha ri bha'i ring Ia sman pa ra si rtas
blangs/

ris blangs/
ge sar du rgyal po dpa" bo'i ring la sman pa rigs bzang
bus blangs/

tshe mgo rmong s nas/ dug gdon gzed du rtags nas 'bor ba'i sman
pa skyes la ma smin pa snyigs dus kyi lo thog Ita bur gyur pa'i
skyon dang (f. 95r) mkhas par khas ches pa rnams kyang gleg bam
la itas rgya che bas kha bshad tsam ma rtogs/ 'chad brtsom gyi
bag chags ma sad pas mkhas pa'i bstan bcos kyi don lta bzhog/ tshig
gi sbyor ba tsam yang ma rtogs pa dang/ gzhung lugs kyi tshig don
la 'khrul pa med kyang/ rgya cher gsungs pa rnams legs par ma
stogs re/ na lugs la spags pa'i sman sbyor khol ba las ji bzhin
ma bgrod pas lan cing/ kho bo ni rigs gnas 'di la skye ba du mar
sbyangs pa'i bag chags rims sad dang/ gzhon nu nyid nas slab
sbyangs phul du phyin pa'i mthus gso dpyad kyi gzhung lugs kun
gsal la ma 'dres pa dngul chu lag mthil du bzhag pa itar rtogs
pa'i don gyi gzhung lugs kun gyi bcud bsdus gso rig dgos pa kun
byung bsam 'phel dbang rgyal 'di/ rang nyid kyi rigs dang rus
la nyams pa med pa'i zhon nu nor bu dpal 'byor mchod sogs phyi
rabs blo gros dang ldan pa'i 'gro don nus pa mnams la gdams re/
dper na rgyud bzhi'i gleng glong ltar ro/
/'dis gzhung lugs la bsre slad kyi gzo lums byas pas skyon
du mi gyur te/ rgyud bzhi 'dir rags pa'i dbang du gleng gzhi sogs
bkod pa'i ston pas gsungs pa ltar 'chad kyang/ phra bar skyes bu
rnams tshe'i snyigs ma mthar thug drug bcu kha ral dus/ lus can

pa'i rgyal po 'gro mgon gyu thog pa nyid kyis gsungs shing/
de yang ding sang tshe lo lnga bcu kha ral mthar thug pa'i skye

de nyid kyi thugs kyi byin rlabs zhugs pa bdag nyid kyis bgyis te
tha mi dad na/ ci ste bsre slad kyi skyon du 'gyur te dper na bsdu
ba po'i (f. 95v) 'khor bzhi ltar ro/
/de Ita bu'i log pa'i skyon dang bral ba'i bstan bcos thams

te/ dper na btso bsreg gi gser bzhin no/

/gso dpyad mtha' yas rgya mtsho las/

Medical works: colophons: Nyi-ma-rnam-rgyal MS.
phan grog sha (broken) sbyar mdzad/ le lha mams snying gi mched
grogs bi shwa'i sprul pa mthong ba don ldan mdzad pa'brug chos
legs no doon byung/ mkhyen pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su gang ba bsam
pa lhun grub kyi le lha kha sha (broken) yi ge 'dri ba dang zhus
dag (bkra shis bsam 'phel gyi kyang) sogs rog ram yang dag mdzad
cing/ ma dpe na sdebs cung ma dag pa mnams khungs idan gyi dag
yig gzhir bzhag nas/ sgo gsum dga' zhing spro ba'i thog nas/ bdag
'gro ba'i 'tsho..(broken) sprang sman khos chung sman sgom bsam
pa don grub kyi lo lnga bcu lnga gcig la pho brang chen po sle
chen dpal mkhar rab brtan lha rtse sogs su 7 gong ma steng zhal
rnams kyi zhabs phyi zhu bzhin sug bris bgyis pa 'dis kyang
rgyal bstan rin po che spyi dang/ khyad par gso ba rig pa'i bstan
pa phyogs dus thams cad du dar zhing rgyas la yun ring du gnas
nas nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i 'gro ba ma lus pa'i srog
'tsho'i boud len chen po mi zad pa'i gter chen po dpag bsam gyi
shing dang bum pa bzang po yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che dgos
'dod kun 'byung lta bur gyur cig/ sarba mangga lam/

The work of four disciples of Si-tu Chos-kyi-' byung-gnas.

min pa'i ga bur rang gi 'byung khungs zur pa yod pa mngon/ tshig

for TSAN DAN DKAR PO ni mdog ser shas can dri shin tu bzang ba
thod pa sogs la gtug na shin tu bsil ba'i nyams yod pa de yin/
'di la ming ba glang mog go shrirşa ha ri ljon pa/ sbrul snying
sa mchog sogs rigs dang ming gi mam grangs 'di sa 'og nas song
ba lo stong lon pa la du ru ka zer ba yin/
TSAN DAN DMAR PO ni smug nag shin tu mkhreg pa su ru tsan
dan ra khrag ma zer ba bzang/ de mtshungs mdog dmar po smug
zhad med cing mkhreg pa so ma tsan dan ste rigs gnyis las med
pa 'khrul so chung/ deng song blun po mams kyi lugs bal po'i
shing dmar phreng ba byed pa 'di shin tu som pa de tsan dmar
by ed pa ni gor tsan yin pas nus pa phyed mtshungs (f. 10r)
tsam yang med par mkhyen gzigs nas gsungs/
de A GA RU la rigs gsum ste ici ba ni a ste/ bsil ba ni rgya
gar nas 'byung ba'i ar skya sob pa/ snum pa ni nag po rgya nag
nas 'byung ba'i rwa co 'dra ba a gar bzang ngan me la dris zhes
pa me la bsregs na gu gul ltar zhu 'gro ba de mchog/ ming 'ba'
zhig zer ba yin/ rgya gar gyi chu klung ka be ra sogs su yod
pa'i shing lo sdong nag po can de la ar nag zer ba de dngos yin/
'di rgya nag pas sbrul snying zer bsil sman du 'dod/
NA GA GE SAR la sdong po la a gu ra zhes grags pa'i shing
rgan po'i snying ar nag khyad par can 'byung/ rgya kar nag gang
nas kyang 'byung ba'i a sam a gu ru zhes grags pa'i shing rgan
po'i snying ar nag 'dra ba de bdug pas gdon byer/ ar nag dngos
ni de mams ma byung na btsan rgod ri bkra sogs rong chen nas
(f. 10v) 'byung ba dang yul gang nas kyang 'ong ba'i shog shing
a gu ru zhes grags pa'i lo ma'i dbyibs ha lam sur dkar 'dra ba
'di gnyis sa rong che chung gi khyad ma gtogs pas tshabs nges
par chog/

Ar-nag
Gi-wam
AR NAG rgya gar nas 'byung ba 'di la'ang ar skya chu nang
du bcug nas smin bcug pa'i bcos ma'ang yod gsungs/ sngo a ga ru
brag dang sa khreb sogs su skye ba'i phung po che la yal ga lang
pa'i rtser me tog sngon po rgyal ba'i spyan can 'dra ba dri zhim
pa gting pa nag po shing 'dra ba de ni dngos yin/
GI WAM ni glang po che re gnyis la yod pa las kun la yod pa
min/ bsags long ra mga phran 'bri lug sogs 'ga' rer la yod pas
ba lang dang ra la la ' byung ba bzang/ mdzo pho mo sogs mga
phran las byung ba der mtshungs/ 'bri byung 'bring/ lug byung ni
mdog kyang dkar po yin pa de ni dman pas btang mi nyan/ (1. llr)
blun po mnams kyis glang chen kho na las 'byung bar sems nas
glang chen gi wam zer yang gi'u wam zhes glang bcud la 'jug/
sa gi wam zer ba 'di ni a tsa ras ba lang gi wam yod pa de shes
nas de btags te phyin la khad par snod du chu bzhag pas ba lang
de skam pas gaung nas kha chu la nye bar phyogs pa de'i kha chu
ser sor chur bab pa der sbru ba'i phyir sa ser po 'jam po btab
pa yin pas nus pa che chung ma gtogs phyogs mtshungs yin/
CU GANG ni gangs ti se sogs nas "byung ba dang/ da ita sa
phugs brag phug sogs nas 'byung ba gnyis ni sa cu gang ste don
gcig ste 'di yang ser shas yod pa bzang/ bang sha ro tsa na zhes
smyug las 'byung ba rgya nag nas 'ong ba'i nag ngam yod pa de
smyug rkang ma ste mchog/ sngo cu gang zer ba rdza 'dabsu sogs
su me tog dkar po rbub 'dra ba de byed pa ni tshod gtam yin pas
'khrul/ angos ni sro lo dkar po (f. 11v) yin pas nus pa mtshungs/
GURGUM ni kha che gurgum zer ba'i dmar smug sha snyam 'dra
ba shin tu khrob pas grug 'gro ba de ni khu ba la bton pa xin pas
mchog/ bal po gur gum mdog dmar ser leb rgan tsi'ang zer ba de

bal gur dang mtshungs/ rtsa kha sdom skabs kha che ma gtogs phyi
ma gnyis kyi go mi chod/

GLA RTSI ni sdog po gcig 'dril ba ni rab/ rdog gnyis gsum Gla-rtsi
du bye ba 'bring/ rtsi nyob dman/ spyir 'di ni rtsi ma gi (or:
ga) ta zer ba nad gdon kun gyis gnyen po bdud rtsi mngon sum
yin pas gzhan mdo rgyud sogs las bshad/ dgu sbyor sogs la dgos
pa'i gla rtsi nag po ni kong po sogs rong chen la yod pa'i gla
ba nag po gzugs ring bong tsam pa shing gi mgo la 'gro ba de'i
rtsi byung na bzang/
DOM MKHRIS (f. 12v) ni gser mkhris g.yu mkhris zer ba ston/ Dom-mkhris
dgun gyi mkhris pa gser mkhris zer ba bzang/ dbyar g.yu mkhris
yin pas dman/ chu la ka btsug zer ba ni ston gyi mkhris pa phal
cher gyis btsugs pas mi 'byed/ mkhris pa med pa'i kha'i shun
pa skam po de 'phur bas mkhris pa gzhan chags 'gro/ dom mkhris
dngos ni rgyus pa bshad pa ltar 'gro/ ma 'byor na khyi nag
snying dkar 'og yod shin tu ngar ba'i mkhris pas tshab chog/
ba lu kha/ rtsa sdom/ khrag good mams ming gi rnam grangs/
'brong mkhris yang tshabs rung/

sbub pa/ g.yu thog pas utpal sngon po rta'i dam dam 'dra gsungs

/gla rtis dug srin mkhal mchin gnyan nad sel/

Inā ga puspa nā ga ge sar dang/

zi ra dkar pos glo yi tshad pa sel/
zi ra nag pos mchin pa'i grang ba sel/
/1a la phud kyis pho nad grang ba sel/
so ma ra dzas lpags nad chu ser sel/
7thal ka rdo rje dag kyang de bzhin no/
7.gser gyi me tog snod tshad mkhris tshad sel/

dug mo nyung gis mkhris sel cha 'khru gcod/
7rgun 'brum glo nad sel zhing tshad pa sbyong/
Zu sus pho ba'i bad kan tsha ba sel]

/bse yab bad kan tsha ba sel bar byed/

me drod skyed cing bad kan grang nad 'joms/

/pi pi ling gis grang nad ma lus sel/

sga skyas bad rlung sel zhing khrag 'khyags 'ju/

ma mu tse yis srin nad sel bar byed/

de la rigs inga rnam rgyal 'jigs med dang/

mnam par rgyal ba ku ba'i mjug ma 'dra/

Bshad rgyud: 20th chapter
/ba ru ra yis bad mkhris chu ser sel/
7skyu mu ra yis bad mkhris khrag nad sel/
snying dang mkhal ma gla gor zho sha gsum
snying tshad mkhal tshad mcher tshal sel bar byed
Za bras sra 'bras jam 'bras mkhal nad sel/
Z'bra gos bad kan smug ser pho nad sel/
(bzhi yu chi ba'i bzhi)
ma nu pa tras rlung khrag tsha ba sel/
Zpuska ra mū las bad kan tsha ba sel/
Zru rtas rlung khrag pho ba sbos pa sel/
Zglo nad gag pa sha ro gcod par byed/
yung bas dug sel rul good gnyan nad 'joms/
/shu dag ma zhu drod skyed gag lhog (f. 27r) sel/
/pu shel skyugs good bad kan tsha ba sel/
khyung sder dkar smug dug tshad sel bar byed/
/dpa' bo dkar ser dpa' rgod de bzhin no/
Zbong nga dkar pos rims dug mkhris tshad sel/
/bong nga dmar ser sha dug btsan dug sel/
/shing mngar glo nad rtsa nad sel bar byed/
sle tres kanda ka ris rlung tshad sel/
Zga bra dag kyang de bzhin rims la phan/
/tig tas mkhris pa'i tshad pa ma lus sel/
ba sha ka yis khrag tshad ma lus sel/
Zba le ka yis glo mchin snod tshad sel/
7ga dur rims dang glo tshad rtsa tshad sel/
stab seng rus chag sbyor zhing rus tshad sel/
(rtsis zhun)
chu
sgron shing bad rlung,ser grang ba sel/

seng Ideng khrag dang chu ser skem par byed/

/dan rog, shri khanda drag por sbyong/
(se nung)

/'khru ba'i nad rams tsha grang med par gcod/
VII. Sngo sman
/sngo yi sman gyi nus pa bstan pa ni/
Thong len khrag skem 'khrugs tshad don tshad sel/
/spang rtsi do bos rims dug mnyings tshad sel/
/re skon khrag skem smug po rtsa tshad sel/
Akyi lces snod tshad mkhris tshad sel bar byed/
Zsum cu tig gis mchid mkhris tsha ba sel/
/pri yangku yis pho mchin tsha ba sel/
zangs tig lcags tig mkhris pa'i tsha ba sel/
Zsro lo sug 'dras glo yi tshad pa sel/
1g.ya' kýi ma yis mkhris pa zhi sbyong byed/
Igang ga chung gis dug dang tshad 'khru gcod/
/bya rgod spos kyis gdon dug rims nad sell
srol gong ba yis mgo chag dug tshad sel/
Zyu mo mde 'byin pu ro zug rngu 'byin/
Zdar ya kan gyis byang khog chu sel skem/
mgo bo'i rus chag sbyor zhing lha ba 'dzin/
Zrta Ipags lha ba 'dzin zhing chu ser 'dren/
la bi sha yis mgo chag dug tshad sel/
stag shas rma 'brub gnyan gsod dug nad sel/
/spang rgyan akar pos gre ba dug tshad sel,
7yu gu (f. 27v) shing gis rma sbyor dug tshad sel/
Irtsad dang rgu thub ldum stag dug nad sel/
la byag ngo chag gso zhing chu se skem/
